# Production Quality Checklist (Core + AI Components)

## Quality Gate (Must Pass)

- Interaction states: hover / active / focus / disabled / loading / error / empty (as applicable)
- Keyboard behavior: complete and deterministic
- Accessibility: semantic roles, labels, `aria-*` wiring, dismiss paths
- Edge behavior: controlled/uncontrolled behavior and close policy clarity
- Tests: unit coverage for key interaction branches
- Storybook: at least one API story + one state/edge scenario story

## Ongoing Maintenance Rules

1. Any API change must update Storybook controls/docs and at least one interaction test.
2. Any a11y behavior change must update role/name assertions in tests.
3. Any visual state change should be checked in all 4 theme packs and Chromatic (if token configured).
4. Release blocking condition: `pnpm verify` + `pnpm coverage:gate` + `pnpm demo:e2e` + `pnpm demo:dist:check` + `pnpm storybook:test:ci` + `pnpm release:dry-run` all green (or run `pnpm release:gate`).

## Recent Closure Notes (2026-03-17)

- CommandPalette: added `Home/End` keyboard paths, deterministic disabled-option skipping, explicit `aria-disabled` option semantics, and query telemetry + empty message Storybook example.
- CommandPalette: live region narration now differentiates visible vs actionable results (`enabledCount`), and announces disabled-only matches as non-executable.
- Toast: live region now wires `aria-labelledby/aria-describedby` by default and supports `ariaLabel` override for icon-only titles.
- Tabs: added `orientation` API with vertical ArrowUp/ArrowDown flow while preserving Home/End and disabled-tab skipping.
- Table: fallback row key now uses source index (not sorted index) so row DOM/state remains stable across sort toggles.
- Dropdown: typeahead now supports buffered multi-character matching, repeated-key cycling, and accent-normalized `textValue` search.
- Dialog: close path now restores focus to the previously focused element by default, with `restoreFocus={false}` escape hatch.
- Dialog overflow parity: modal surface now constrains max viewport height and enables inner content scrolling for long-copy flows.
- Toast close-button state parity: close control now aligns hover/active/focus-visible feedback with tokenized interaction styling.
- Toast close lifecycle parity: manual close now suppresses timeout duplicate callbacks in the same open cycle.
- Toast escape-stack parity: when top toast disables Escape, dismissal now falls through to the nearest escapable toast.
- Release dry-run package discovery parity: publish dry-run now auto-discovers non-private packages under `packages/*` and records skipped/no-package state in summary.
- Release preflight scope parity: `release:preflight` now supports `--scope=all|chromatic|publish`, matching optional Chromatic vs required publish validation workflows.
- Table live-region parity: empty datasets now suppress sort-status live narration so empty-state messaging remains single-source.
- Token integrity parity: added `--aurora-color-amber-500` to global tokens so warning-tone Progress/Empty no longer depend on undefined CSS vars.
- Drawer close-button parity: close control now matches Dialog/Toast hover/active/focus-visible treatment for overlay-level interaction consistency.
- Tabs idref parity: tab/panel `id` wiring now stays stable even when `items[].key` contains spaces, symbols, or non-Latin text.
- Demo productization parity: page shell now uses full-viewport themed background, and hero navigation/KPI cards expose clearer hover + focus-visible hierarchy.
- Storybook docs gate parity: docs check now validates both `*Stories` imports and `of={XStories.Y}` export existence before interaction runner.
- Toast timer continuity parity: hover/focus pauses now resume auto-dismiss with remaining time instead of resetting full duration.
- Chromatic gate parity: workflow now supports soft-skip (default) and enforce hard-fail mode (`workflow_dispatch` + `enforce=true`) for release audits.
- Chromatic summary parity: skip/fail branches now emit the same summary fields as upload runs (`status`, `build/storybook url`, `change/error count`) with `n/a` placeholders for missing token cases.
- Table natural-sort parity: sortable string columns now use `Intl.Collator` for numeric/case-friendly ordering (`a2 < A10 < A11`).
- Tabs key-boundary parity: non-applicable arrow keys are now explicitly covered by regression tests (no focus or panel drift).
- CommandPalette lint parity: option click path now carries keyboard listener fallback to satisfy strict a11y lint gates.
- Demo label parity: KPI card semantics no longer collide with theme-select accessible label queries in E2E/assistive tooling.
- Release gate recovery parity: after fixing CommandPalette lint + demo label collision, `release:gate:ci` returned to full-pass state on 2026-03-19.
- Feedback token parity: Alert/Toast/Badge now share tokenized `feedback.*` palette instead of component-local hardcoded rgba/hex colors.
- CommandPalette focus model hardening: option nodes now stay out of tab order (`tabIndex=-1`) and preserve combobox focus on pointer selection for `aria-activedescendant` parity.
- CommandPalette search hardening: `commands[].textValue` now supports non-string labels, and matching is accent-insensitive (`cafe` matches `CafГ©`).
- Table i18n hardening: `getSortAriaLabel` now enables localized sortable-header narration while preserving `aria-sort` behavior.
- Table loading hardening: `loading/loadingContent` now sets `aria-busy`, suppresses stale rows/empty-state rendering, and disables sort controls during refresh windows.
- Table row-key diagnostics hardening: development builds now warn when `rowKey` returns duplicate values, reducing silent row-identity collisions in sorted/interactive tables.
- Table row-key hardening: `rowKey(row, rowIndex)` now receives source-data index (not sorted visual index), preventing index-derived key churn during sort toggles.
- Table render-index hardening: `columns[].render(row, rowIndex, sourceIndex)` now exposes visual index + source index together, so sorted rankings and source-linked telemetry can stay deterministic.
- Table header semantics hardening: non-sortable columns no longer expose `aria-sort`, preventing screen readers from announcing inert headers as sortable.
- Toast stack-order hardening: Escape dismissal now targets only the latest open toast first, so stacked notifications close deterministically from top to bottom.
- Toast interaction-priority hardening: focusing or hovering an older toast now promotes it to stack top so Escape follows current user interaction context.
- CommandPalette batching hardening: `closeOnSelect` now supports persistent mode for multi-command execution without repeated reopen friction.
- Tabs naming hardening: `ariaLabelledBy` now supports visible-heading-linked tablist naming, reducing generic screen-reader labels.
- Popover/Dropdown dismiss-policy hardening: both overlays now expose `closeOnEscape` / `closeOnOutsidePointer` and low-level dismiss event hooks for blocking confirmation flows.
- CommandPalette dismiss-policy hardening: palette now supports `closeOnEscape` / `closeOnOutsidePointer` toggles for approval flows that must stay open until explicit action.
- Demo CommandPalette blocking-mode coverage: added UI toggle for dismiss policy (`closeOnEscape/closeOnOutsidePointer`) and Playwright regression asserting Escape/outside click do not close when blocking mode is enabled.
- Demo Toast blocking-mode coverage: added `closeOnEscape={false}` notification path and Playwright regression asserting Escape is ignored until explicit close action.
- Demo CommandPalette persistent-mode coverage: added runtime `closeOnSelect=false` toggle and Playwright regression asserting selection keeps palette open for batch actions.
- Demo CommandPalette disabled-option coverage: added disabled archive command and Playwright regression asserting click does not close or execute blocked action.
- Demo Toast stack-order coverage: added runtime stacked-toast trigger and Playwright regression asserting Escape closes newest toast before older notices.
- Demo Tabs manual-activation coverage: added `activationMode="manual"` data-workflow example and Playwright regression locking focus-move vs Enter-activation split.
- Demo Tabs vertical-orientation coverage: added `orientation="vertical"` example and Playwright ArrowUp/ArrowDown regression for focus + activation flow.
- Demo Table loading coverage: added runtime loading toggle and Playwright regression for `aria-busy`, disabled sort controls, and stale-row suppression.
- Demo Table empty-state coverage: added runtime empty toggle and Playwright regression asserting empty copy plus disabled sortable headers.
- Demo Dropdown focus-policy coverage: added outside-focus target and Playwright regressions for Escape trigger focus return + outside pointer focus retention.
- Demo Dropdown Tab flow coverage: added Playwright regression asserting menu closes on Tab and focus continues to the next actionable control.
- Storybook Dropdown focus-policy coverage: added explicit `EscapeDismissFocusReturn` interaction scenario to lock trigger focus restoration on keyboard dismiss.
- Storybook docs parity: `Component API` and `Best Practices` now both include Dropdown focus-policy canvases for implementation + QA alignment.
- CommandPalette disabled-action guard: added dedicated Storybook `DisabledCommandGuard` interaction scenario plus unit branch to ensure disabled options never execute and never dismiss palette.
- Toast Escape preemption guard: added Storybook `EscapePreemptedByGlobalHandler` scenario to lock `defaultPrevented` semantics and prevent accidental dismiss under global shortcut handlers.
- Table keyboard sort parity: added `Enter/Space` activation coverage in unit + Storybook `SortTelemetry` play assertions to lock non-pointer sorting flows.
- Tabs keyboard edge parity: Storybook `KeyboardNavigationGuide` now includes `Home/End` assertions with disabled-tab skipping to lock focus/selection semantics.
- Data API docs parity: Component API + Best Practices now explicitly document Table sortable-header keyboard activation (`Enter/Space`) for integration teams.
- Demo data-flow parity: Playwright now covers Table sort keyboard activation (`Enter`/`Space`) to match Storybook/unit keyboard sorting guarantees.
- Demo tabs parity: Playwright now covers manual-activation `Space` path so Enter/Space semantics stay aligned with Tabs API contract.
- Tabs cross-browser keyboard parity: manual activation now accepts legacy `Spacebar` key value, with dedicated unit regression coverage.
- Tabs keyboard parity extension: manual activation now also accepts modern `Space` key value, and Storybook manual-flow interactions explicitly validate the Space activation path.
- Tabs panel-focus parity: active `tabpanel` now exposes `tabIndex=0` while inactive panels stay `-1`, ensuring keyboard users can reliably enter panel content.
- Tabs removal fallback hardening: when the currently selected tab is removed at runtime, uncontrolled tabs now fall back to the nearest enabled tab by historical index (instead of always jumping to first), with unit + Storybook interaction coverage.
- Tabs telemetry de-dup hardening: manual mode now ignores follow-up keyboard-generated click (`detail=0`) after key activation, preventing duplicate `onValueChange` emissions.
- Tabs keyboard-discoverability hardening: manual mode now exposes `aria-keyshortcuts="Enter Space"` on tabs, with unit + Storybook interaction coverage.
- Demo Tabs keyboard-discoverability parity: Playwright manual-mode flows now assert `aria-keyshortcuts="Enter Space"` on actionable tabs.
- Tabs activation-repeat parity: manual mode now ignores repeated activation keydown (`Enter` / `Space`, `event.repeat=true`) so long-press does not emit duplicate value-change telemetry.
- Storybook Tag stability hardening: `Core/Tag/MetadataRow` now has explicit play assertions to reduce interaction-runner navigation retry noise.
- Storybook Toast stability hardening: `Feedback/Toast/ToneMatrix` now uses `duration={0}` so baseline stories stay deterministic during interaction-runner sweeps.
- Storybook Pagination stability hardening: keyboard stories now await async role transitions (`findByRole`) and assert focus preconditions to reduce interaction-runner retry noise.
- Pagination naming hardening: added `ariaLabelledBy` so pager nav can inherit visible-heading naming and suppress fallback `aria-label` when heading binding is present.
- Pagination focus-continuity hardening: keyboard paging (`Home/End/Arrow`) now restores focus to the newly active page button, with unit + Storybook interaction coverage.
- Pagination Arrow-focus regression coverage: added explicit unit assertions for `ArrowLeft/ArrowRight` focus handoff so keyboard page transitions keep focus anchored to the newly active page.
- Pagination boundary hardening: `pageCount<=1` now short-circuits before token/range math, with regression coverage for `0` and negative page counts.
- Storybook static-sync gate hardening: `storybook:static:check` now rebuilds static output and fails on `git status` diff so stale static artifacts are blocked before interaction tests.
- Storybook docs parity hardening: added `storybook:docs:parity:check` to enforce shared component import coverage between `Component-API.mdx` and `Best-Practices.mdx`, then wired it into `storybook:test:ci`.
- Storybook play-coverage gate hardening: `storybook:play:check` now enforces at least one `play` interaction per `*.stories.*` file, with `MessageBubble` interactive assertionиЎҘйҪҗеҲ° 32/32 story files.
- Storybook a11y gate hardening: `@storybook/test-runner` now executes `axe-playwright` in `preVisit/postVisit`, and `color-contrast` is scoped to a tracked story-id skip list instead of global disable.
- Storybook color-contrast debt reduction: Badge/Tag contrast styles were hardened and related skip-list entries (`core-badge--tone-matrix`, `core-badge--ai-interaction-status`, `core-tag--ai-context-markers`) removed from test-runner exemptions.
- Storybook skip-list governance gate: added `storybook:a11y:skip-check` to enforce skip-id dedup/order/existence against `storybook-static/index.json`, preventing stale or drifting a11y exemptions.

- Button keyboard parity: added legacy `Spacebar` activation-key compatibility regression for pressed-state feedback.
- Button loading/disabled state parity: pressed visual offset now clears immediately when runtime transitions to `loading` or `disabled`.
- Button focus-visible parity: focus ring now appears only for keyboard-visible focus and stays hidden for pointer-driven focus paths.
- Form invalid-token parity: `aria-invalid=\"grammar|spelling\"` now remains intact across Input/Select/Textarea/DatePicker/Checkbox/RadioGroup/Switch/FormField instead of collapsing to `true`.
- Input placeholder-token parity: `data-aurora-input` + global `::placeholder` style now activates `--aurora-input-placeholder` consistently across themes.
- FormField invalid precedence parity: field-level `error` now explicitly overrides child `aria-invalid=\"grammar|spelling\"` to `true`, keeping form-error narration deterministic.
- Storybook invalid-token parity: added `Form/Input/InvalidTokenSemantics` play assertion to keep `aria-invalid=\"grammar\"` semantics inside visual/interaction regression chain.
- Tabs interaction hardening: `activationMode="manual"` decouples arrow-key focus movement from activation and supports Enter/Space commit.
- Toast escape hardening: Escape now respects `defaultPrevented` so stacked notifications close one at a time.
- Overlay focus-policy hardening: Popover/Dropdown now restore trigger focus on Escape while preserving outside pointer target focus on pointer dismiss.
- Overlay scroll-lock hardening: Dialog/Drawer now share reference-counted body scroll lock, preventing premature unlock when multiple modal surfaces overlap.
- DismissableLayer stack hardening: nested overlays now dismiss from top layer first on Escape/outside pointer, preventing multi-layer cascade closes.
- Overlay non-primary pointer hardening: right-click/non-primary pointerdown now no longer dismisses overlays, with Dialog/Drawer/Popover/Dropdown/CommandPalette regression coverage locking the branch.
- Demo non-primary pointer parity: Playwright now validates Dialog/Drawer/Popover/Dropdown/CommandPalette remain open on right-click/outside non-primary pointer, aligning E2E behavior with overlay unit guardrails.
- Dialog nested overlay coverage: added `Dropdown in Dialog` Escape-order test + Storybook scenario to lock top-layer-first dismissal behavior.
- Drawer nested overlay coverage: added `Dropdown in Drawer` Escape-order test + Storybook scenario to lock one-layer-per-Escape dismiss behavior.
- Drawer focus-return parity: added `restoreFocus` API + unit/storybook interaction coverage to align close-focus policy with Dialog defaults.
- Release dry-run refresh: `pnpm release:dry-run` revalidated on 2026-03-18 with publishable tarballs (`tokens ~3.0 kB`, `primitives ~13.9 kB`, `react ~50.0 kB`).

- FormField иҜӯд№үеҗҲе№¶дҝ®еӨҚпјҡдҝқз•ҷеӯҗжҺ§д»¶ж—ўжңү `aria-describedby/aria-invalid/required`пјҢе№¶дёҺеӯ—ж®өзә§жҸҗзӨә/й”ҷиҜҜеҒҡеўһйҮҸеҗҲе№¶гҖӮ
- FormField required/error ж”¶еҸЈпјҡ`aria-required="false"` дёҚеҶҚиў«иҜҜеҲӨдёәеҝ…еЎ«пјҢдё”еӯҗжҺ§д»¶ `aria-errormessage` дјҡдёҺеӯ—ж®өй”ҷиҜҜ ID еҺ»йҮҚеҗҲе№¶гҖӮ
- Tag/Badge иҰҶзӣ–иЎҘйҪҗпјҡж–°еўһеҚ•жөӢе№¶жҺҘе…Ҙ Storybook `Core/Tag` + `Core/Badge` еңәжҷҜпјҢиЎҘдёҠеҜјеҮәз»„д»¶йӘҢж”¶й—ӯзҺҜгҖӮ
- Verify иҙЁйҮҸй—ЁзҰҒдҝ®еӨҚпјҡPagination й”®зӣҳеҝ«жҚ·й”®ж”№дёәжҢүй’®зә§еӨ„зҗҶд»Ҙж»Ўи¶і a11y lintпјҢRadioGroup `aria-invalid` ж”¶ж•ӣеҲ° `radiogroup` е®№еҷЁпјҢTooltip/Storybook зӨәдҫӢиЎҘйҪҗ lint еҗҲи§„еҶҷжі•гҖӮ
- CommandPalette еҸҜи®ҝй—®жҖ§иЎҘејәпјҡж–°еўһеҸҜе®ҡеҲ¶з»“жһңж’ӯжҠҘ `getResultsStatusText`пјҢе°Ҷз©әзҠ¶жҖҒеҸҜи§Ҷж–ҮжЎҲдёҺ live region и§ЈиҖҰпјҢиЎҘйҪҗеҚ•жөӢдёҺ Storybook йҒҘжөӢеңәжҷҜгҖӮ
- Core з»„д»¶еӣһеҪ’иЎҘзӮ№пјҡдёә `Core/Tag` дёҺ `Core/Badge` еўһеҠ  Storybook `play` ж–ӯиЁҖпјҢзЎ®дҝқзҠ¶жҖҒж–ҮжЎҲиҝӣе…Ҙи§Ҷи§ү/дәӨдә’еӣһеҪ’й“ҫи·ҜгҖӮ
- FormField ж–ҮжЎЈж”¶еҸЈпјҡж–°еўһ `Form/FormField` Storybook е…ҘеҸЈдёҺ `play` ж–ӯиЁҖпјҢиЎҘйҪҗеӯҗжҺ§д»¶ `aria-describedby` / `aria-errormessage` еҗҲе№¶зҡ„еҸҜжү§иЎҢзӨәдҫӢгҖӮ
- Table е‘ҪеҗҚиҜӯд№үиЎҘйҪҗпјҡж–°еўһ `ariaLabel` API дёҺ Storybook `AccessibleNameWithoutCaption` еңәжҷҜпјҢиҰҶзӣ–ж—  caption зҡ„еҸҜи®ҝй—®жҖ§еҲҶж”ҜгҖӮ
- Table е‘ҪеҗҚиҜӯд№үжү©еұ•пјҡж–°еўһ `ariaLabelledBy` API дёҺ Storybook `AccessibleNameLabelledByHeading` еңәжҷҜпјҢиҰҶзӣ–еҸҜи§Ғж Үйўҳе‘ҪеҗҚиЎЁж ји·Ҝеҫ„е№¶дјҳе…ҲдәҺ `ariaLabel`гҖӮ

- Tabs еӣһи°ғиҜӯд№үж”¶еҸЈпјҡйҮҚеӨҚзӮ№еҮ»е·ІйҖүдёӯйЎөзӯҫдёҚеҶҚи§ҰеҸ‘ `onValueChange`пјҢе№¶иЎҘйҪҗ Storybook йҒҘжөӢеҺ»йҮҚдәӨдә’ж–ӯиЁҖгҖӮ

- Dropdown typeahead ж”¶еҸЈпјҡж–°еўһеӯ—жҜҚй”®и·іиҪ¬дёҺзҰҒз”ЁйЎ№и·іиҝҮпјҢж”ҜжҢҒ `textValue` дёәйқһеӯ—з¬ҰдёІж ҮзӯҫжҸҗдҫӣеҢ№й…Қж–Үжң¬гҖӮ

- Storybook зұ»еһӢй—ЁзҰҒдҝ®еӨҚпјҡ`FormField` story еўһиЎҘй»ҳи®Ө `args`пјҢжҒўеӨҚ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/storybook-app typecheck` е…Ёз»ҝгҖӮ

- Table activation-repeat parity: sortable headers now ignore repeated activation keydown (`event.repeat=true`) for `Enter` / `Space` so keyboard long-press does not generate duplicate sort toggles/telemetry.
- Table loading-sort semantics parity: loading mode now clears header `aria-sort` so assistive tech does not announce stale sorted state while rows and sort controls are non-interactive.
- Table loading-label parity: when sort state exists, loading mode now preserves sortable-header next-direction label (`aria-label`) while keeping controls disabled and `aria-sort` suppressed.
- CommandPalette activedescendant parity: combobox now sanitizes active option references during query/command updates so `aria-activedescendant` never points to missing or disabled options.
- CommandPalette empty-result activedescendant parity: when filtering yields no results, combobox now clears `aria-activedescendant` and restores it only after valid options return, with unit + Storybook `EmptyStateAriaControlsLifecycle` coverage.
- Demo section-nav parity: `activeSection` now tracks viewport sections via `IntersectionObserver`, so hero cards and nav pills stay aligned during scroll (not only hash changes).
- Gate observability parity: CI/Release workflows now upload Storybook/Demo/Release gate raw logs as artifacts and include Storybook coverage issue counters in summaries for faster triage.
- Demo interaction-state parity: section nav and hero stat cards now use CSS state selectors (`:hover`, `:focus-visible`, `[aria-current]`) instead of component-local hover/focus state machines.
- Demo reduced-motion parity: `prefers-reduced-motion` now disables transform-driven nav/card motion, preserving readability for motion-sensitive users.

- Popover/Dropdown йқһж–Үжң¬и§ҰеҸ‘еҷЁе…ңеә•е‘ҪеҗҚж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+306пјүпјҡPopover дёҺ Dropdown еңЁйқһж–Үжң¬и§ҰеҸ‘еҷЁдё”жңӘжҸҗдҫӣ `triggerAriaLabel/triggerAriaLabelledBy` ж—¶ж–°еўһ `aria-label` е…ңеә•пјҲ`Open popover` / `Open menu`пјүпјҢйҒҝе…ҚеҮәзҺ°ж— еҗҚжҢүй’®пјӣеҗҢж—¶дҝқз•ҷејҖеҸ‘жҖҒзјәеӨұе‘ҪеҗҚе‘ҠиӯҰд»Ҙеј•еҜјжҳҫејҸиҜӯд№үеЈ°жҳҺпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Popover.tsx`гҖҒ`Dropdown.tsx`гҖҒеҜ№еә”еҚ•жөӢдёҺ Storybook `NonTextTriggerAutoNameFallback` еңәжҷҜпјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Popover.test.tsx src/Dropdown.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Popover.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Dropdown.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ

- ReasoningPanel еҲҮжҚўжҢүй’®ж ҮйўҳдёҠдёӢж–Үе‘ҪеҗҚж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+316пјүпјҡReasoningPanel й»ҳи®Ө `expand/collapse` ж Үзӯҫж”№дёәиҮӘеҠЁйҷ„еҠ еҸҜиҜ» `title` дёҠдёӢж–ҮпјҲеҰӮ `Expand reasoning panel: Model reasoning`пјүпјҢйҒҝе…ҚеӨҡйқўжқҝеңәжҷҜиҜ»еұҸеҗҢеҗҚеҶІзӘҒпјӣдҝқз•ҷиҮӘе®ҡд№ү `expandLabel/collapseLabel` еҺҹж ·иҫ“еҮәпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `ReasoningPanel.tsx`гҖҒ`ReasoningPanel.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `Default` дёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/ReasoningPanel.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "ReasoningPanel.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- StreamingCodeBlock еҮҸе°‘еҠЁж•ҲеҒҸеҘҪиҜӯд№үж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+317пјүпјҡStreamingCodeBlock ж–°еўһ `respectReducedMotion`пјҲй»ҳи®Ө `true`пјүпјҢеңЁзі»з»ҹеҗҜз”Ё reduced-motion ж—¶иҮӘеҠЁйҖҖеҢ–дёәеҚіж—¶е®Ңж•ҙжёІжҹ“пјҢйҒҝе…Қеӯ—з¬Ұзә§жөҒејҸеҠЁз”»йҖ жҲҗеҠЁж•ҲиҙҹжӢ…пјӣж”ҜжҢҒ `respectReducedMotion=false` жҳҫејҸжҒўеӨҚжөҒејҸеҠЁз”»пјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `StreamingCodeBlock.tsx`гҖҒ`StreamingCodeBlock.test.tsx` дёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/StreamingCodeBlock.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "StreamingCodeBlock.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- PromptInput жҸҗдәӨеҝ«жҚ·й”®йҳІжҠ–дёҺе®ҝдё»еҝ«жҚ·й”®е…је®№ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+318пјүпјҡPromptInput еңЁ `Ctrl/Cmd + Enter` жҸҗдәӨи·Ҝеҫ„ж–°еўһ `event.repeat` йҳІйҮҚеӨҚжҸҗдәӨдёҺ `Alt + Ctrl/Cmd + Enter` е®ҝдё»еҝ«жҚ·й”®ж—Ғи·ҜпјҢжҸҗдәӨжҲҗеҠҹж—¶жҳҫејҸ `event.preventDefault()` йҒҝе…Қ textarea жҚўиЎҢеүҜдҪңз”ЁпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `PromptInput.tsx`гҖҒ`PromptInput.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `WithAiRequestState`гҖҒComponent API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/PromptInput.test.tsx`пјҲ`18/18`пјүгҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "PromptInput.stories.tsx"`пјҲ`8/8`пјүгҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ

- PromptInput ж— жҸҗдәӨеӨ„зҗҶеҷЁеҸҜз”ЁжҖ§иҜӯд№үж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+330пјүпјҡPromptInput еңЁжңӘжҸҗдҫӣ `onSubmit` ж—¶ж”№дёәиў«еҠЁиҜӯд№үпјҢеҸ‘йҖҒжҢүй’®дҝқжҢҒзҰҒз”ЁгҖҒ`Ctrl/Cmd + Enter` дёҚеҶҚиў«з»„д»¶жӢҰжҲӘгҖҒ`aria-keyshortcuts` дёҺеҝ«жҚ·й”®жҸҗзӨәдёҚеҶҚиҜҜеҜјжҡҙйңІпјҢд»ҺиҖҢйҒҝе…ҚвҖңиҫ“е…Ҙиў«жё…з©әдҪҶж— жҸҗдәӨеҠЁдҪңвҖқзҡ„иҜҜиЎҢдёәпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `PromptInput.tsx`гҖҒ`PromptInput.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `WithoutSubmitHandler` еңәжҷҜдёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/PromptInput.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "PromptInput.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- CommandPalette ж— еӨ„зҗҶеҷЁе‘Ҫд»ӨйҖүжӢ©йҳІиҜҜе…іж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+331пјүпјҡCommandPalette йҖүжӢ©йЎ№еңЁжңӘжҸҗдҫӣ `onSelect` ж—¶дёҚеҶҚи§ҰеҸ‘е…ій—ӯй“ҫи·ҜпјҢйҒҝе…ҚвҖңж— еҠЁдҪңе‘Ҫд»Өиў«жү§иЎҢе№¶е…ій—ӯйқўжқҝвҖқзҡ„иҜҜеҲӨпјӣиЎҘйҪҗ `CommandPalette.test.tsx` еӣһеҪ’дёҺ Storybook `MissingSelectHandlerGuard` еңәжҷҜпјҢе№¶еҗҢжӯҘ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/CommandPalette.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "CommandPalette.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Toast йқһдәӨдә’ action и§’иүІдёҺжҢҒд№…еҢ–иҜӯд№үж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+332пјүпјҡToast д»…еңЁ `action` еҗ«дәӨдә’иҠӮзӮ№ж—¶еҚҮзә§дёә `dialog/alertdialog` дё”й»ҳи®ӨжҢҒд№…еҢ–пјӣзәҜж–Үжң¬/ж•°еӯ— action ж”№дёәдҝқз•ҷеҶ…е®№еұ•зӨәдҪҶз»ҙжҢҒ `status/alert` иў«еҠЁиҜӯд№үдёҺй»ҳи®Өи¶…ж—¶зӯ–з•ҘпјҢйҒҝе…ҚвҖңж— еҸҜжү§иЎҢеҠЁдҪңеҚҙиў«еҲӨе®ҡдёәдәӨдә’ toastвҖқзҡ„иҜҜеҲӨпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Toast.tsx`гҖҒ`Toast.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `TextActionSemantics` еңәжҷҜдёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Toast.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Toast.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Table ж— жҺ’еәҸеңәжҷҜж»ҡеҠЁе®№еҷЁй”®зӣҳеҸҜиҫҫжҖ§ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+333пјүпјҡTable еңЁж— еҸҜж“ҚдҪңжҺ’еәҸжҺ§д»¶ж—¶пјҢе°Ҷж»ҡеҠЁе®№еҷЁж”¶еҸЈдёә `role="region" + tabIndex=0 + aria-keyshortcuts`пјҢе№¶иЎҘйҪҗ `ArrowLeft/ArrowRight/Home/End/PageUp/PageDown` й”®зӣҳжЁӘеҗ‘ж»ҡеҠЁпјҢйҒҝе…ҚвҖңд»…еҸҜиҒҡз„ҰдҪҶж— жі•й”®зӣҳе№із§»жәўеҮәеҲ—вҖқзҡ„дјӘеҸҜиҫҫй—®йўҳпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Table.tsx`гҖҒ`Table.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `KeyboardReachableScrollContainer` дёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Table.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Table.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Tabs е…ЁзҰҒз”ЁеңәжҷҜй”®зӣҳеҸ‘зҺ°жҖ§ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+334пјүпјҡTabs еңЁжүҖжңү `items` еқҮзҰҒз”Ёж—¶пјҢдёә `tablist` иҮӘеҠЁиЎҘ `tabIndex=0` еӣһйҖҖз„ҰзӮ№е…ҘеҸЈпјҢйҒҝе…Қз»„д»¶иў«й”®зӣҳйЎәеәҸе®Ңе…Ёи·іиҝҮеҜјиҮҙвҖңзҰҒз”ЁзҠ¶жҖҒдёҚеҸҜеҸ‘зҺ°вҖқпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Tabs.tsx`гҖҒ`Tabs.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `AllTabsDisabled` дёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Tabs.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Tabs.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Table ж»ҡеҠЁе®№еҷЁйў„еҚ дҪҚй”®зӣҳдјҳе…Ҳзә§йӘҢж”¶иЎҘйҪҗпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+335пјүпјҡиЎҘйҪҗвҖңдёҠеұӮ `preventDefault()` йў„еҚ дҪҚж—¶дёҚи§ҰеҸ‘ж»ҡеҠЁе®№еҷЁ Arrow/Home/End/Page й”®зӣҳе№із§»вҖқзҡ„еҚ•жөӢдёҺ Storybook дәӨдә’ж–ӯиЁҖпјҢй”Ғе®ҡ host shortcut guard дјҳе…Ҳзә§пјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Table.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `KeyboardReachableScrollContainer` дёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Table.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Table.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Demo Data еҸҜеҸ‘зҺ°жҖ§дёҺй”®зӣҳе№із§»еңәжҷҜиЎҘйҪҗпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+336пјүпјҡDemo Data еҢәеҹҹж–°еўһ `All disabled release workflow tabs` дёҺ `Non-sortable readiness snapshot` дёӨдёӘжҲҗе“ҒеҢ–еңәжҷҜпјҢеүҚиҖ…йӘҢиҜҒе…ЁзҰҒз”Ё tabs зҡ„ fallback з„ҰзӮ№е…ҘеҸЈпјҢеҗҺиҖ…йӘҢиҜҒж— жҺ’еәҸиЎЁж јж»ҡеҠЁеҢәеҹҹ Arrow/Home/End/Page й”®зӣҳе№із§»пјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `apps/demo/src/main.tsx`гҖҒ`apps/demo/src/main.css`гҖҒ`e2e/demo.spec.ts` е№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm demo:e2e:grep "all-disabled tabs discoverable|supports keyboard panning in non-sortable"` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Toast action дәӨдә’еҲӨе®ҡиҜӯд№үж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+337пјүпјҡToast `action` иҜӯд№үеҲӨе®ҡз”ұвҖңд»»ж„Ҹ React е…ғзҙ еҚідәӨдә’вҖқж”¶еҸЈдёәвҖңд»…еҸҜдәӨдә’жҺ§д»¶/иҜӯд№үиҠӮзӮ№жүҚеҚҮзә§ dialogвҖқпјҢдҝ®еӨҚ `<span>ж–Үжң¬</span>` иў«иҜҜеҲӨдёәдәӨдә’ toast зҡ„и§’иүІдёҺжҢҒд№…еҢ–еҒҸе·®пјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Toast.tsx`гҖҒ`Toast.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `TextActionSemantics` дёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Toast.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Toast.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Dropdown е…ЁзҰҒз”ЁиҸңеҚ•з„ҰзӮ№й”ҡзӮ№ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+338пјүпјҡDropdown еңЁ `items` е…ЁзҰҒз”Ёж—¶пјҢиҸңеҚ•еұ•ејҖеҗҺиҮӘеҠЁе°Ҷз„ҰзӮ№й”ҡе®ҡеҲ° menu surfaceпјҲ`tabIndex=-1`пјүпјҢйҒҝе…Қй”®зӣҳжү“ејҖи·Ҝеҫ„еҒңз•ҷеңЁ trigger еҜјиҮҙвҖңиҸңеҚ•е·Іеұ•ејҖдҪҶж— з„ҰзӮ№дёҠдёӢж–ҮвҖқпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Dropdown.tsx`гҖҒ`Dropdown.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `AllItemsDisabledKeyboardNoop` дёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Dropdown.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Dropdown.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- CommandPalette disabled-only еҸҜи§ЈйҮҠжҸҗзӨәж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+339пјүпјҡCommandPalette ж–°еўһ `disabledResultsMessage`пјҢеңЁвҖңжңүеҢ№й…Қз»“жһңдҪҶеқҮдёҚеҸҜжү§иЎҢвҖқеңәжҷҜжҳҫзӨәеҸҜи§Ғи§ЈйҮҠж–ҮжЎҲпјҢе№¶е°Ҷе…¶е№¶е…Ҙ combobox `aria-describedby`пјҢйҒҝе…Қз”ЁжҲ·д»…и§ҒзҰҒз”ЁйЎ№еҚҙдёҚжё…жҘҡдёҚеҸҜжү§иЎҢеҺҹеӣ пјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `CommandPalette.tsx`гҖҒ`CommandPalette.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `DisabledOnlyResults` дёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/CommandPalette.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "CommandPalette.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Toast еҸҜиҒҡз„Ұ action дәӨдә’иҜӯд№үж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+340пјүпјҡToast `action` дәӨдә’еҲӨе®ҡиЎҘйҪҗ `tabIndex>=0` еҸҜиҒҡз„ҰиҠӮзӮ№еҲҶж”ҜпјҢдҝ®еӨҚвҖңеҸҜиҒҡз„Ұ action иў«иҜҜеҲӨдёәиў«еҠЁеҶ…е®№вҖқеҜјиҮҙи§’иүІжңӘеҚҮзә§дёҺй»ҳи®Өи¶…ж—¶зӯ–з•Ҙй”ҷиҜҜзҡ„й—®йўҳпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Toast.tsx`гҖҒ`Toast.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `TextActionSemantics` дёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Toast.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Toast.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Table ж»ҡеҠЁеҝ«жҚ·й”®жҸҗзӨәжәўеҮәжҖҒж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+341пјүпјҡTable еңЁвҖңж— еҸҜж“ҚдҪңжҺ’еәҸжҺ§д»¶вҖқеҲҶж”ҜдёӢпјҢ`aria-keyshortcuts` ж”№дёәд»…еңЁеӯҳеңЁжЁӘеҗ‘жәўеҮәж—¶жҡҙйңІпјҢйҒҝе…ҚйқһжәўеҮәеёғеұҖдёӢеҗ‘иҜ»еұҸ/QA й”ҷиҜҜе®Јз§°еҸҜз”Ёзҡ„ж»ҡеҠЁеҝ«жҚ·й”®пјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Table.tsx`гҖҒ`Table.test.tsx`гҖҒComponent API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Table.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Table.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Tabs е…ЁзҰҒз”ЁйқўжқҝеҸҜи§ҒжҖ§ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+342пјүпјҡTabs еңЁжүҖжңү tab disabled ж—¶ж”№дёәдҝқз•ҷеҪ“еүҚ/йҰ–дёӘйқўжқҝеҸҜи§ҒпјҢйҒҝе…ҚвҖңзҠ¶жҖҒзҰҒз”ЁеҚіеҶ…е®№е…Ёз©әвҖқзҡ„дҪ“йӘҢж–ӯеұӮпјӣеҗҢж—¶зҰҒз”Ё tab з»ҹдёҖз»ҙжҢҒ `tabIndex=-1`пјҢе№¶иЎҘйҪҗе…ЁзҰҒз”Ё rerender еҲҶж”ҜеҚ•жөӢдёҺ Storybook `AllTabsDisabled` йӘҢж”¶пјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Tabs.tsx`гҖҒ`Tabs.test.tsx`гҖҒ`Tabs.stories.tsx` дёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Tabs.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Tabs.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Dropdown еҜјиҲӘй”®йў„еҚ дҪҚж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+343пјүпјҡDropdown еңЁеҸҜж“ҚдҪңйЎ№ `<=1` ж—¶дёҚеҶҚжӢҰжҲӘ Arrow/Home/End/Page еҜјиҲӘй”®пјҢйҒҝе…Қж— еҸҜеҜјиҲӘеҲҶж”ҜеҗһжҺүе®ҝдё»й»ҳи®Өй”®зӣҳиЎҢдёәпјӣдҝқжҢҒеҝ«жҚ·й”®жҸҗзӨәдёҺеҸҜжү§иЎҢиЎҢдёәдёҖиҮҙпјҲд»… `Tab/Escape`пјүпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Dropdown.tsx`гҖҒ`Dropdown.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `AllItemsDisabledKeyboardNoop` / `SingleActionableShortcutHints` дёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Dropdown.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Dropdown.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- CommandPalette icon-only е‘Ҫд»Өе‘ҪеҗҚеӣһйҖҖж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-22 latest+344пјүпјҡCommandPalette еңЁ non-text label дё”зјәеӨұ `ariaLabel/ariaLabelledBy` ж—¶ж–°еўһ `textValue` е‘ҪеҗҚе…ңеә•пјҢйҒҝе…ҚеҮәзҺ°ж— еҗҚ optionпјӣејҖеҸ‘жҖҒзјәеӨұе‘ҪеҗҚе‘ҠиӯҰеҗҢжӯҘеҚҮзә§дёә `ariaLabel/ariaLabelledBy/textValue` дёүйҖүдёҖпјҢе№¶иЎҘйҪҗ `CommandPalette.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `IconOnlyCommandTextValueFallback` дёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/CommandPalette.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "CommandPalette.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ

- RadioGroup з»„зә§зҰҒз”ЁиҜӯд№үж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+358пјүпјҡRadioGroup еңЁ `disabled` еңәжҷҜдёә `radiogroup` е®№еҷЁиЎҘйҪҗ `aria-disabled="true"`пјҢзЎ®дҝқ assistive tech еҸҜж„ҹзҹҘз»„зә§дёҚеҸҜз”ЁзҠ¶жҖҒпјҲдёҚеҶҚд»…дҫқиө–еҚ•дёӘ radio зҡ„ disabledпјүпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `RadioGroup.tsx`гҖҒ`RadioGroup.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `GroupDisabledSemantics` еңәжҷҜдёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/RadioGroup.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "RadioGroup.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- RadioGroup е‘ҪеҗҚ/жҸҸиҝ°иҜӯд№үжӢҶеҲҶж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+359пјүпјҡRadioGroup йҖүйЎ№жҸҸиҝ°д»ҺеҸҜи®ҝй—®еҗҚз§°дёӯжӢҶеҲҶпјҢж”№дёә `aria-describedby` дё“иҒҢиҫ…еҠ©иҜҙжҳҺпјҢдҝқиҜҒ radio еҗҚз§°зЁіе®ҡдё”з®ҖжҙҒпјӣеҗҢж—¶ејҖеҸ‘жҖҒвҖңйқһж–Үжң¬ label зјәеӨұжҳҫејҸе‘ҪеҗҚвҖқе‘ҠиӯҰдёҚеҶҚиў« description ж–Үжң¬иҜҜе…ңеә•гҖӮеҗҢжӯҘ `RadioGroup.tsx`гҖҒ`RadioGroup.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `NumericDescriptionSemantics` еңәжҷҜдёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/RadioGroup.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "RadioGroup.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Checkbox е‘ҪеҗҚ/жҸҸиҝ°иҜӯд№үжӢҶеҲҶж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+360пјүпјҡCheckbox е‘ҪеҗҚй“ҫи·Ҝж”№дёәвҖң`label`/жҳҫејҸ aria е‘ҪеҗҚдјҳе…ҲпјҢ`description` д»…иө° `aria-describedby`вҖқпјҢдҝ®еӨҚжҸҸиҝ°ж–ҮжЎҲж··е…ҘеҸҜи®ҝй—®еҗҚз§°еҜјиҮҙиҜ»еұҸеҗҚз§°еҶ—й•ҝзҡ„й—®йўҳпјӣејҖеҸ‘жҖҒвҖңйқһж–Үжң¬ label зјәеӨұжҳҫејҸе‘ҪеҗҚвҖқе‘ҠиӯҰеҗҢжӯҘдёҚеҶҚиў« description ж–Үжң¬иҜҜе…ңеә•гҖӮеҗҢжӯҘ `Checkbox.tsx`гҖҒ`Checkbox.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `NumericContentSemantics` еңәжҷҜдёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Checkbox.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Checkbox.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Switch йқһж–Үжң¬е‘ҪеҗҚе‘ҠиӯҰзІҫеәҰж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+361пјүпјҡSwitch ејҖеҸ‘жҖҒе‘ҪеҗҚе‘ҠиӯҰж”№дёәд»…еҹәдәҺ `label` ж–Үжң¬еҸҜиҜ»жҖ§еҲӨе®ҡпјҢ`description` дёҚеҶҚиҜҜдҪңдёәе‘ҪеҗҚжқҘжәҗпјҢдҝ®еӨҚвҖңеӣҫж Ү label + ж–Үжң¬ descriptionвҖқеңәжҷҜжјҸе‘ҠиӯҰй—®йўҳе№¶дёҺ `aria-labelledby + aria-describedby` иҜӯд№үдёҖиҮҙпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Switch.tsx`гҖҒ`Switch.test.tsx`пјҲж–°еўһ description-only е‘ҪеҗҚзјәеҸЈеӣһеҪ’пјүдёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Switch.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Switch.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Input жң¬ең°й”®зӣҳйў„еҚ дҪҚдјҳе…Ҳзә§ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+362пјүпјҡInput `onKeyDown` еӣһи°ғжү§иЎҢйЎәеәҸеүҚзҪ®пјҢдҝқиҜҒдёҡеҠЎдҫ§жң¬ең° `event.preventDefault()` еҸҜйҳ»ж–ӯ Enter active еҸҚйҰҲпјҢдҝ®еӨҚвҖңжң¬ең° guard е·Ійў„еҚ дҪҚдҪҶд»ҚеҮәзҺ° `data-active`вҖқзҡ„дёҚдёҖиҮҙиЎҢдёәпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Input.tsx`гҖҒ`Input.test.tsx`пјҲж–°еўһ local preempt еӣһеҪ’пјүгҖҒStorybook `ManagedKeysPreemptedByLocalHandler` еңәжҷҜдёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Input.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Input.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Button жң¬ең°й”®зӣҳйў„еҚ дҪҚдјҳе…Ҳзә§ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+363пјүпјҡButton `onKeyDown` еӣһи°ғжү§иЎҢйЎәеәҸеүҚзҪ®пјҢдҝқиҜҒдёҡеҠЎдҫ§жң¬ең° `event.preventDefault()` еҸҜйҳ»ж–ӯжҢүеҺӢеҸҚйҰҲпјҢдҝ®еӨҚвҖңжң¬ең° guard е·Ійў„еҚ дҪҚдҪҶд»ҚеҮәзҺ° `translateY(1px)` pressed и§Ҷи§үвҖқзҡ„дёҚдёҖиҮҙиЎҢдёәпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Button.tsx`гҖҒ`Button.test.tsx`пјҲж–°еўһ local preempt еӣһеҪ’пјүгҖҒStorybook `ManagedKeysPreemptedByLocalHandler` еңәжҷҜдёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Button.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Button.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Toast е…ій—ӯжҢүй’®жң¬ең°йў„еҚ дҪҚдјҳе…Ҳзә§ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+364пјүпјҡToast ж–°еўһ `onCloseButtonKeyDown` й’©еӯҗе№¶еүҚзҪ®жү§иЎҢпјҢзЎ®дҝқдёҡеҠЎдҫ§жң¬ең° `event.preventDefault()` еҸҜйҳ»ж–ӯе…ій—ӯжҢүй’® pressed еҸҚйҰҲпјҢдҝ®еӨҚвҖңжң¬ең° guard е·Ійў„еҚ дҪҚдҪҶд»ҚеҮәзҺ° `translateY(1px)`вҖқзҡ„дёҚдёҖиҮҙиЎҢдёәпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Toast.tsx`гҖҒ`Toast.test.tsx`пјҲж–°еўһ local preempt еӣһеҪ’пјүгҖҒStorybook `CloseButtonManagedKeysPreemptedByLocalHandler` еңәжҷҜдёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Toast.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Toast.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- CommandPalette жң¬ең°жҢүй”®йў„еҚ дҪҚдјҳе…Ҳзә§ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+365пјүпјҡCommandPalette ж–°еўһ `onSearchKeyDown` й’©еӯҗе№¶еүҚзҪ®жү§иЎҢпјҢдҝқиҜҒдёҡеҠЎдҫ§жң¬ең° `event.preventDefault()` еҸҜйҳ»ж–ӯ `Enter/Escape` з®ЎзҗҶй”®еӨ„зҗҶпјҢдҝ®еӨҚвҖңжң¬ең° guard е·Ійў„еҚ дҪҚдҪҶд»Қи§ҰеҸ‘е‘Ҫд»Өжү§иЎҢжҲ– query clearвҖқзҡ„дёҚдёҖиҮҙиЎҢдёәпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `CommandPalette.tsx`гҖҒ`CommandPalette.test.tsx`пјҲж–°еўһ local preempt еӣһеҪ’пјүгҖҒStorybook `ManagedKeysPreemptedByLocalHandler` еңәжҷҜдёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/CommandPalette.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "CommandPalette.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Tabs жң¬ең°жҢүй”®йў„еҚ дҪҚдјҳе…Ҳзә§ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+366пјүпјҡTabs ж–°еўһ `onTabKeyDown` й’©еӯҗе№¶еүҚзҪ®жү§иЎҢпјҢдҝқиҜҒдёҡеҠЎдҫ§жң¬ең° `event.preventDefault()` еҸҜйҳ»ж–ӯ roving focus дёҺ manual activation з®ЎзҗҶй”®еӨ„зҗҶпјҢдҝ®еӨҚвҖңжң¬ең° guard е·Ійў„еҚ дҪҚдҪҶд»Қи§ҰеҸ‘ Arrow еҜјиҲӘжҲ– Enter жҝҖжҙ»вҖқзҡ„дёҚдёҖиҮҙиЎҢдёәпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Tabs.tsx`гҖҒ`Tabs.test.tsx`пјҲж–°еўһ local preempt еӣһеҪ’пјүгҖҒStorybook `ManagedKeysPreemptedByLocalHandler` еңәжҷҜдёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Tabs.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Tabs.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Table жң¬ең°жҢүй”®йў„еҚ дҪҚдјҳе…Ҳзә§ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+367пјүпјҡTable ж–°еўһ `onSortKeyDown` й’©еӯҗе№¶еүҚзҪ®жү§иЎҢпјҢдҝқиҜҒдёҡеҠЎдҫ§жң¬ең° `event.preventDefault()` еҸҜйҳ»ж–ӯ sortable-header еҜјиҲӘдёҺжҝҖжҙ»з®ЎзҗҶй”®еӨ„зҗҶпјҢдҝ®еӨҚвҖңжң¬ең° guard е·Ійў„еҚ дҪҚдҪҶд»Қи§ҰеҸ‘ Arrow еҲ—еӨҙи·іиҪ¬жҲ– Enter жҺ’еәҸвҖқзҡ„дёҚдёҖиҮҙиЎҢдёәпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Table.tsx`гҖҒ`Table.test.tsx`пјҲж–°еўһ local preempt еӣһеҪ’пјүгҖҒStorybook `ManagedSortKeysPreemptedByLocalHandler` еңәжҷҜдёҺ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Table.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:build`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Table.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check && pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check && pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Demo жң¬ең°жҢүй”®йў„еҚ дҪҚйӘҢж”¶йқўжқҝж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+368пјүпјҡDemo ж–°еўһ Keyboard Guard LabпјҢйӣҶдёӯеҸҜи§ҶеҢ– Tabs `onTabKeyDown`гҖҒTable `onSortKeyDown`гҖҒCommandPalette `onSearchKeyDown`гҖҒToast `onCloseButtonKeyDown` еӣӣжқЎжң¬ең°йў„еҚ дҪҚй’©еӯҗпјҢжҸҗдҫӣ guard ејҖе…ідёҺ telemetryпјҲ`tabs-local-guard-telemetry`гҖҒ`table-local-guard-telemetry`гҖҒ`table-local-sort-telemetry`гҖҒ`palette-local-key-guard-telemetry`гҖҒ`toast-close-button-guard-telemetry`пјүж”Ҝж’‘дёҡеҠЎй”®зӣҳжҠӨж ҸйӘҢж”¶пјӣеҗҢжӯҘж–°еўһ Playwright еӣһеҪ’иҰҶзӣ–вҖңguard ејҖеҗҜйҳ»ж–ӯ / е…ій—ӯжҒўеӨҚвҖқеӣӣзұ»и·Ҝеҫ„пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm demo:build`гҖҒ`pnpm demo:e2e:grep "local onTabKeyDown guard|local onSortKeyDown guard|local search key guard|close button Enter via local key guard"` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Tooltip и§ҰеҸ‘еҷЁж–Үжң¬зұ»еһӢй—ЁзҰҒж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+369пјүпјҡдҝ®еӨҚ Tooltip и§ҰеҸ‘еҷЁ `children` еңЁзұ»еһӢж”¶зӘ„й“ҫи·Ҝдёӯиў«жҺЁж–ӯдёә `unknown` еҜјиҮҙ demo typecheck еӨұиҙҘзҡ„й—®йўҳпјӣеңЁеҸҜиҜ»ж–Үжң¬жҺўжөӢи·Ҝеҫ„жҳҫејҸеҜ№ `children` жү§иЎҢ `ReactNode` иҜӯд№үж”¶зӘ„пјҢзЎ®дҝқ `getReadableTooltipTextNode` и°ғз”ЁдёҺ TypeScript й—ЁзҰҒдёҖиҮҙгҖӮеҗҢжӯҘеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/demo typecheck`гҖҒ`pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Tooltip.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Tooltip.stories.tsx"` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Storybook зұ»еһӢй—ЁзҰҒйҳ»еЎһж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+370пјүпјҡдҝ®еӨҚ `@aurora-ui/storybook-app` typecheck йҳ»еЎһй“ҫи·Ҝпјҡ`Alert/Empty` з»„д»¶ props ж”№дёә `Omit<ComponentPropsWithoutRef<"div">, "title">` йҒҝе…ҚиҮӘе®ҡд№ү `title: ReactNode` иў«еҺҹз”ҹ `title: string` дәӨеҸүзӘ„еҢ–пјӣ`StoryShowcaseFrame` иЎҘйҪҗ `align` ж”ҜжҢҒеҜ№йҪҗж—ўжңүж•…дәӢз”Ёжі•пјӣ`CommandPalette/Popover/Tooltip` ж•…дәӢиЎҘйҪҗиҫ“е…Ҙзұ»еһӢж”¶зӘ„дёҺзјәеӨұ `args`пјҢжҒўеӨҚ CSF зұ»еһӢе®Ңж•ҙжҖ§гҖӮеҗҢжӯҘеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/storybook-app typecheck`гҖҒ`pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Alert.test.tsx src/Empty.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "(Alert|Empty|CommandPalette|Popover|Tooltip).stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm typecheck` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Combobox Enter й•ҝжҢүеҺ»йҮҚж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+371пјүпјҡCombobox еңЁй”®зӣҳйҖүжӢ©и·Ҝеҫ„ж–°еўһ `event.repeat` йҳІйҮҚе…ҘеӨ„зҗҶпјҢдҝ®еӨҚй•ҝжҢү Enter еҜјиҮҙйҮҚеӨҚ `onValueChange` дёҺиҜҜе…ій—ӯжҠ–еҠЁйЈҺйҷ©пјӣеҗҢжӯҘиЎҘйҪҗ `Combobox.test.tsx` йҮҚеӨҚ Enter еӣһеҪ’гҖҒStorybook `ModifierKeyGuard` йҮҚеӨҚ Enter дәӨдә’ж–ӯиЁҖпјҢд»ҘеҸҠ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈй”®зӣҳеҘ‘зәҰиҜҙжҳҺгҖӮеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Combobox.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Combobox.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Demo Combobox й•ҝжҢү Enter еӣһеҪ’ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+372пјүпјҡPlaywright ж–°еўһ `ignores repeated Enter keydown before combobox selection commit`пјҢй”Ғе®ҡвҖң`event.repeat=true` дёҚеә”иҜҜйҖүдёӯ/иҜҜе…ій—ӯпјҢйҰ–дёӘйқһ repeat Enter жүҚжҸҗдәӨйҖүжӢ©вҖқз«ҜеҲ°з«ҜеҘ‘зәҰпјӣеҗҢжӯҘеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm demo:e2e:grep "ignores repeated Enter keydown before combobox selection commit|selects framework from combobox"` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Combobox жң¬ең°й”®зӣҳйў„еҚ дҪҚй’©еӯҗж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+373пјүпјҡCombobox ж–°еўһ `onInputKeyDown` е№¶еүҚзҪ®жү§иЎҢпјҢж”ҜжҢҒдёҡеҠЎдҫ§йҖҡиҝҮ `event.preventDefault()` жӢҰжҲӘ Arrow/Home/End/Enter/Escape з®ЎзҗҶй”®пјӣеҗҢжӯҘиЎҘйҪҗ `Combobox.test.tsx` жң¬ең° guard еӣһеҪ’гҖҒStorybook `ManagedKeysPreemptedByLocalHandler` дәӨдә’ж•…дәӢпјҢд»ҘеҸҠ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„гҖӮеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Combobox.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Combobox.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Demo Combobox жң¬ең°й”®зӣҳ guard йӘҢж”¶ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+374пјүпјҡDemo еңЁ Framework Combobox еңәжҷҜж–°еўһжң¬ең° guard ејҖе…ідёҺ telemetryпјҲ`combobox-local-key-guard-telemetry`пјүпјҢз”ЁдәҺеҸҜи§ҶеҢ–йӘҢиҜҒ `onInputKeyDown + preventDefault()` йў„еҚ дҪҚиЎҢдёәпјӣеҗҢжӯҘж–°еўһ Playwright з”ЁдҫӢ `preempts combobox Enter selection via local key guard hook`пјҢй”Ғе®ҡвҖңguard ејҖеҗҜйҳ»ж–ӯ Enter жҸҗдәӨпјҢе…ій—ӯеҗҺжҒўеӨҚжҸҗдәӨвҖқз«ҜеҲ°з«ҜеҘ‘зәҰгҖӮеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm demo:e2e:grep "preempts combobox Enter selection via local key guard hook|selects framework from combobox"` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Dialog/Drawer е…ій—ӯжҢүй’®жң¬ең°й”®зӣҳйў„еҚ дҪҚж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+375пјүпјҡDialog дёҺ Drawer ж–°еўһ `onCloseButtonKeyDown` й’©еӯҗе№¶еүҚзҪ®жү§иЎҢпјҢж”ҜжҢҒдёҡеҠЎдҫ§йҖҡиҝҮ `event.preventDefault()` йҳ»ж–ӯ Enter/Space зҡ„е…ій—ӯжҢүй’® pressed еҸҚйҰҲпјҢдҝ®еӨҚвҖңжң¬ең° guard е·Ійў„еҚ дҪҚдҪҶд»Қи§ҰеҸ‘ `translateY(1px)`вҖқзҡ„дёҚдёҖиҮҙиЎҢдёәпјӣеҗҢжӯҘ `Dialog.tsx`гҖҒ`Drawer.tsx`гҖҒ`Dialog.test.tsx`гҖҒ`Drawer.test.tsx`пјҲж–°еўһ local preempt еӣһеҪ’пјүгҖҒStorybook `CloseButtonManagedKeysPreemptedByLocalHandler` еңәжҷҜпјҢд»ҘеҸҠ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„гҖӮеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Dialog.test.tsx src/Drawer.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/storybook-app typecheck`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Dialog.stories.tsx|Drawer.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Demo Dialog/Drawer е…ій—ӯжҢүй’®жң¬ең°й”®зӣҳ guard йӘҢж”¶ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+376пјүпјҡDemo Overlay Dismiss Telemetry йқўжқҝж–°еўһ Dialog/Drawer жң¬ең°й”®зӣҳ guard ејҖе…ідёҺ telemetryпјҲ`dialog-close-button-guard-telemetry`гҖҒ`drawer-close-button-guard-telemetry`пјүпјҢе№¶е°Ҷ `onCloseButtonKeyDown + preventDefault()` жҺҘе…Ҙзңҹе®һ overlay е®һдҫӢпјҢж”ҜжҢҒз«ҜеҲ°з«ҜеҸҜи§ҶеҢ–йӘҢиҜҒвҖңејҖеҗҜйҳ»ж–ӯ Enter/SpaceгҖҒе…ій—ӯеҗҺжҒўеӨҚй»ҳи®Өе…ій—ӯвҖқпјӣеҗҢжӯҘж–°еўһ Playwright еӣһеҪ’з”ЁдҫӢ `preempts dialog close button Enter via local key guard hook` дёҺ `preempts drawer close button Enter via local key guard hook`пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/demo typecheck`гҖҒ`pnpm demo:e2e:grep "preempts dialog close button Enter via local key guard hook|preempts drawer close button Enter via local key guard hook"`гҖҒ`pnpm demo:build` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- CommandPalette е…ій—ӯжҢүй’®жң¬ең°й”®зӣҳйў„еҚ дҪҚж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+377пјүпјҡCommandPalette ж–°еўһ `onCloseButtonKeyDown` е№¶йҖҸдј  Dialog е…ій—ӯжҢүй’®й”®зӣҳй“ҫи·ҜпјҢж”ҜжҢҒдёҡеҠЎдҫ§йҖҡиҝҮ `event.preventDefault()` йў„еҚ дҪҚ Enter/Space close-button жҢүй”®еӨ„зҗҶпјӣеҗҢжӯҘиЎҘйҪҗ `CommandPalette.test.tsx` жң¬ең° preempt еӣһеҪ’гҖҒStorybook `CloseButtonManagedKeysPreemptedByLocalHandler` дәӨдә’ж•…дәӢпјҢд»ҘеҸҠ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„гҖӮеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/CommandPalette.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/storybook-app typecheck`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "CommandPalette.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check`гҖҒ`pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react lint` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Demo CommandPalette е…ій—ӯжҢүй’®жң¬ең°й”®зӣҳ guard йӘҢж”¶ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+378пјүпјҡDemo Command Palette Policy Controls йқўжқҝж–°еўһ close-button guard ејҖе…ідёҺ telemetryпјҲ`palette-close-button-guard-telemetry`пјүпјҢе№¶е°Ҷ `onCloseButtonKeyDown + preventDefault()` жҺҘе…Ҙзңҹе®һ `CommandPalette` е®һдҫӢпјҢж”ҜжҢҒз«ҜеҲ°з«ҜеҸҜи§ҶеҢ–йӘҢиҜҒвҖңејҖеҗҜйҳ»ж–ӯ Enter/SpaceгҖҒе…ій—ӯеҗҺжҒўеӨҚй»ҳи®Өе…ій—ӯвҖқпјӣеҗҢжӯҘж–°еўһ Playwright еӣһеҪ’з”ЁдҫӢ `preempts command palette close button Enter via local key guard hook`пјҢе№¶еӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/demo typecheck`гҖҒ`pnpm demo:e2e:grep "preempts command palette close button Enter via local key guard hook"`гҖҒ`pnpm demo:build` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Demo CommandPalette е…ій—ӯжҢүй’® Space жң¬ең° guard йӘҢж”¶ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+379пјүпјҡPlaywright ж–°еўһ `preempts command palette close button Space via local key guard hook`пјҢиЎҘйҪҗ close-button guard зҡ„ Space еҲҶж”Ҝз«ҜеҲ°з«ҜеҘ‘зәҰпјҢй”Ғе®ҡвҖңguard ејҖеҗҜйҳ»ж–ӯ Space е…ій—ӯгҖҒе…ій—ӯеҗҺжҒўеӨҚй»ҳи®Өе…ій—ӯвҖқиЎҢдёәпјӣеҗҢжӯҘеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm demo:e2e:grep "preempts command palette close button (Enter|Space) via local key guard hook"` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Demo Toast е…ій—ӯжҢүй’® Space жң¬ең° guard йӘҢж”¶ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+380пјүпјҡPlaywright ж–°еўһ `preempts telemetry toast close button Space via local key guard hook`пјҢиЎҘйҪҗ telemetry toast close-button guard зҡ„ Space еҲҶж”Ҝз«ҜеҲ°з«ҜеҘ‘зәҰпјҢй”Ғе®ҡвҖңguard ејҖеҗҜйҳ»ж–ӯ Space е…ій—ӯгҖҒе…ій—ӯеҗҺжҒўеӨҚй»ҳи®Өе…ій—ӯвҖқиЎҢдёәпјӣеҗҢжӯҘеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm demo:e2e:grep "preempts telemetry toast close button (Enter|Space) via local key guard hook"` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Demo Tabs/Table жң¬ең° Space guard йӘҢж”¶ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+381пјүпјҡPlaywright ж–°еўһ `preempts tabs Space activation through local onTabKeyDown guard in lab panel` дёҺ `preempts table sort Space activation through local onSortKeyDown guard in lab panel`пјҢиЎҘйҪҗ Keyboard Guard Lab дёӯ Tabs/Table зҡ„ Space еҲҶж”Ҝз«ҜеҲ°з«ҜеҘ‘зәҰпјҢй”Ғе®ҡвҖңguard ејҖеҗҜйҳ»ж–ӯ Space з®ЎзҗҶй”®гҖҒе…ій—ӯеҗҺжҒўеӨҚй»ҳи®ӨжҝҖжҙ»/жҺ’еәҸвҖқиЎҢдёәпјӣеҗҢжӯҘеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm demo:e2e:grep "preempts tabs (managed keys|Space activation) through local onTabKeyDown guard in lab panel|preempts table sort (activation|Space activation) through local onSortKeyDown guard in lab panel"` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Demo Dialog/Drawer е…ій—ӯжҢүй’® Space жң¬ең° guard йӘҢж”¶ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+382пјүпјҡPlaywright ж–°еўһ `preempts dialog close button Space via local key guard hook` дёҺ `preempts drawer close button Space via local key guard hook`пјҢиЎҘйҪҗ overlay close-button guard зҡ„ Space еҲҶж”Ҝз«ҜеҲ°з«ҜеҘ‘зәҰпјҢй”Ғе®ҡвҖңguard ејҖеҗҜйҳ»ж–ӯ Space е…ій—ӯгҖҒе…ій—ӯеҗҺжҒўеӨҚй»ҳи®Өе…ій—ӯвҖқиЎҢдёәпјӣеҗҢжӯҘеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm demo:e2e:grep "preempts (dialog|drawer) close button (Enter|Space) via local key guard hook"` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Demo Tabs guard жҝҖжҙ»ж–ӯиЁҖзІҫеәҰж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+383пјүпјҡе°Ҷ `preempts tabs managed keys...` дёҺ `preempts tabs Space activation...` з”ЁдҫӢеҚҮзә§дёәвҖңиҒҡз„ҰжңӘйҖүдёӯ Handoff tab еҗҺйӘҢиҜҒ Enter/Space жҝҖжҙ»йҳ»ж–ӯвҖқпјҢдҝ®еӨҚеҺҹе…ҲеңЁе·ІйҖүдёӯ tab дёҠжҢүй”®еҜјиҮҙзҡ„еҒҮйҳіжҖ§и·Ҝеҫ„пјҢзЎ®дҝқ guard йӘҢж”¶зңҹе®һиҰҶзӣ–жҝҖжҙ»иҜӯд№үпјӣеҗҢжӯҘеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm demo:e2e:grep "preempts tabs (managed keys|Space activation) through local onTabKeyDown guard in lab panel"` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Demo е…ій—ӯжҢүй’®й”®зӣҳеҝ«жҚ·жҸҗзӨәеҸҜеҸ‘зҺ°жҖ§ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+384пјүпјҡPlaywright ж–°еўһ `exposes close-button keyboard shortcut hints across overlay and toast surfaces`пјҢз»ҹдёҖйӘҢж”¶ Dialog/Drawer/CommandPalette/Telemetry Toast е…ій—ӯжҢүй’® `aria-keyshortcuts="Enter Space"` жҡҙйңІпјҢй”Ғе®ҡй”®зӣҳеҸҜеҸ‘зҺ°жҖ§еңЁ Demo йӣҶжҲҗеұӮдёҚеӣһйҖҖпјӣеҗҢжӯҘеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm demo:e2e:grep "exposes close-button keyboard shortcut hints across overlay and toast surfaces"` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Demo жң¬ең° guard Space й”®еҗҚе…је®№ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+385пјүпјҡж–°еўһ `normalizeGuardActivationKey` з»ҹдёҖеҪ’дёҖеҢ– `Enter/Space/Spacebar/" "`пјҢдҝ®еӨҚ Demo жң¬ең° guard д»…иҜҶеҲ«з©әж јеӯ—з¬ҰдёҺ `Spacebar`гҖҒйҒ—жјҸ `key="Space"` е…је®№и·Ҝеҫ„зҡ„й—®йўҳпјӣеҗҢжӯҘиҰҶзӣ– Tabs/Table/Dialog/Drawer/CommandPalette/Toast guard й“ҫи·Ҝе№¶ж–°еўһ Playwright еӣһеҪ’ `preempts command palette close button key='Space' alias via local key guard hook`гҖӮеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/demo typecheck`гҖҒ`pnpm demo:e2e:grep "preempts command palette close button (Enter|Space|key='Space' alias) via local key guard hook"` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Demo Tabs/Table `key="Space"` еҲ«еҗҚ guard йӘҢж”¶ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+386пјүпјҡPlaywright ж–°еўһ `preempts tabs key='Space' alias...` дёҺ `preempts table sort key='Space' alias...`пјҢиЎҘйҪҗ Keyboard Guard Lab еҜ№ `key="Space"` еҺҶеҸІй”®еҗҚи·Ҝеҫ„зҡ„з«ҜеҲ°з«ҜеҘ‘зәҰпјҢй”Ғе®ҡ guard telemetry дёҺйҳ»ж–ӯиЎҢдёәеңЁ tabs жҝҖжҙ»/иЎЁж јжҺ’еәҸй“ҫи·ҜдёҖиҮҙз”ҹж•ҲпјӣеҗҢжӯҘеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm demo:e2e:grep "preempts tabs (managed keys|Space activation|key='Space' alias) through local onTabKeyDown guard in lab panel|preempts table sort (activation|Space activation|key='Space' alias) through local onSortKeyDown guard in lab panel"` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- FormField invalid/errormessage иҜӯд№үеҘ‘зәҰж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+387пјүпјҡFormField д»…еңЁ invalid иҜӯд№үжҝҖжҙ»ж—¶жҡҙйңІ `aria-errormessage`пјҲеӯ—ж®өзә§ `error` жҲ–еӯҗжҺ§д»¶е·І invalidпјүпјҢдҝ®еӨҚвҖңеҸҜйҖү/жңүж•ҲжҺ§д»¶д»ҚйҖҸдј  errormessageвҖқиҜӯд№үеҷӘйҹіпјӣеҗҢж—¶ `data-invalid` дёҺеӯҗжҺ§д»¶ invalid иҜӯд№үеҜ№йҪҗпјҢе№¶иЎҘйҪҗ `FormField.test.tsx` еӣһеҪ’гҖҒStorybook `ErrorMessageInvalidContract` дәӨдә’ж•…дәӢпјҢд»ҘеҸҠ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„гҖӮеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/FormField.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "FormField.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- CommandPalette й»ҳи®Өе…ій—ӯж–ҮжЎҲеҸҜи®ҝй—®жҖ§ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+388пјүпјҡCommandPalette й»ҳи®Ө `closeLabel` з”ұжіӣеҢ– `Close dialog` ж”¶ж•ӣдёә `Close command palette`пјҢйҷҚдҪҺе‘Ҫд»ӨйқўжқҝдёҺйҖҡз”ЁеҜ№иҜқжЎҶзҡ„еҸҜи®ҝй—®еҗҚз§°жӯ§д№үпјӣеҗҢжӯҘиЎҘйҪҗ `CommandPalette.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `CommandPalette.stories.tsx`гҖҒDemo E2E е‘Ҫд»Өйқўжқҝе…ій—ӯи·Ҝеҫ„ж–ӯиЁҖпјҢд»ҘеҸҠ Component API ж–ҮжЎЈ fallback ж–ҮжЎҲеҸЈеҫ„гҖӮеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/CommandPalette.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "CommandPalette.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm demo:e2e:grep "command palette|Command Palette"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Dropdown йқһж–Үжң¬и§ҰеҸ‘еҷЁй»ҳи®Өе‘ҪеҗҚж–ҮжЎҲж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+389пјүпјҡDropdown icon-only/non-text trigger еңЁзјәзңҒе‘ҪеҗҚи·Ҝеҫ„зҡ„ fallback ж–ҮжЎҲз”ұ `Open menu` ж”¶ж•ӣдёә `Open dropdown menu`пјҢйҷҚдҪҺдёҚеҗҢиҸңеҚ•/еј№еұӮжҺ§д»¶еңЁиҜ»еұҸзҺҜеўғдёӯзҡ„еҗҚз§°жӯ§д№үпјӣеҗҢжӯҘиЎҘйҪҗ `Dropdown.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `NonTextTriggerAutoNameFallback` ж–ӯиЁҖпјҢд»ҘеҸҠ Component API ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„гҖӮеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Dropdown.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Dropdown.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Popover trigger Tab дҝ®йҘ°й”®е®ҲеҚ«ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+390пјүпјҡPopover еңЁ trigger иҒҡз„Ұдё”йқўжқҝе·Іжү“ејҖж—¶пјҢ`Tab` иҫ№з•Ң dismiss д»…е“Қеә”жңӘдҝ®йҘ°жҢүй”®пјҢ`Ctrl/Meta/Alt + Tab` дёҚеҶҚиҜҜи§ҰеҸ‘е…ій—ӯдёҺз„ҰзӮ№иҝҒз§»пјҢйҒҝе…ҚеҠ«жҢҒжөҸи§ҲеҷЁ/е®ҝдё»еҝ«жҚ·й”®пјӣеҗҢжӯҘиЎҘйҪҗ `Popover.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `TriggerTabModifierGuard` дәӨдә’ж•…дәӢпјҢд»ҘеҸҠ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„гҖӮеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Popover.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Popover.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Dropdown Tab дҝ®йҘ°й”®е…ій—ӯе®ҲеҚ«ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+391пјүпјҡDropdown еңЁ trigger/menu и·Ҝеҫ„зҡ„ `Tab` dismiss д»…е“Қеә”жңӘдҝ®йҘ°жҢүй”®пјҢ`Ctrl/Meta/Alt + Tab` дёҚеҶҚиҜҜи§ҰеҸ‘е…ій—ӯдёҺз„ҰзӮ№иҝҒз§»пјҢйҒҝе…ҚеҠ«жҢҒжөҸи§ҲеҷЁ/е®ҝдё»еҝ«жҚ·й”®пјӣеҗҢжӯҘиЎҘйҪҗ `Dropdown.test.tsx`гҖҒStorybook `TabModifierDismissGuard` дәӨдә’ж•…дәӢпјҢд»ҘеҸҠ Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„гҖӮеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Dropdown.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:test:grep "Dropdown.stories.tsx"`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- FocusScope дҝ®йҘ°й”® Tab дёҺи·Ёж–ҮжЎЈ activeElement ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+392пјүпјҡ`@aurora-ui/primitives` `FocusScope` д»…еҜ№жңӘдҝ®йҘ° `Tab`/`Shift+Tab` жү§иЎҢз„ҰзӮ№еҫӘзҺҜпјҢ`Ctrl/Meta/Alt + Tab` дёҚеҶҚиҜҜи§ҰеҸ‘з„ҰзӮ№йҷ·йҳұпјӣеҗҢж—¶з„ҰзӮ№еҲӨе®ҡж”№дёәеҹәдәҺ `ownerDocument.activeElement`пјҢдҝ®еӨҚ iframe/multi-document е®ҝдё»дёӢеҫӘзҺҜиҫ№з•ҢеҲӨе®ҡжјӮз§»гҖӮеҗҢжӯҘиЎҘйҪҗ `FocusScope.test.tsx`пјҲжңӘдҝ®йҘ°еҫӘзҺҜгҖҒдҝ®йҘ°й”®ж”ҫиЎҢгҖҒiframe ownerDocument и·Ҝеҫ„пјүдёҺ `Dialog.test.tsx`/`Drawer.test.tsx` йӣҶжҲҗеӣһеҪ’пјҢе№¶жӣҙж–° Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„гҖӮеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/primitives exec vitest run src/FocusScope.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Dialog.test.tsx src/Drawer.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
- Tabs з©әжҖҒй”®зӣҳеҒңйқ зӮ№ж”¶еҸЈпјҲ2026-03-23 latest+393пјүпјҡTabs еӣһйҖҖ tab stop зӯ–з•Ҙж”¶зҙ§дёәвҖңиҮіе°‘еӯҳеңЁ tab дё”е…ЁйғЁ disabledвҖқжүҚеңЁ tablist жҡҙйңІ `tabIndex=0`/`aria-disabled`пјҢдҝ®еӨҚ `items=[]` з©әжҖҒд»ҚжҸ’е…Ҙж— ж„Ҹд№үй”®зӣҳеҒңйқ зӮ№зҡ„й—®йўҳпјӣеҗҢжӯҘиЎҘйҪҗ `Tabs.test.tsx` з©әжҖҒеӣһеҪ’пјҲtablist дёҚеҸҜиҒҡз„ҰгҖҒTab йЎәеәҸзӣҙиҫҫеүҚеҗҺжҺ§д»¶пјүе№¶жӣҙж–° Component API / Best Practices ж–ҮжЎЈеҸЈеҫ„гҖӮеӨҚйӘҢ `pnpm --filter @aurora-ui/react exec vitest run src/Tabs.test.tsx`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:parity:check`гҖҒ`pnpm storybook:docs:structure:check` йҖҡиҝҮгҖӮ
